posted:Posted February 9, 2023
msg:Nothing is certain except the location is good. The so-called five-star hotel somehow got it, and it is not up to standard at all. I don't know how the good reviews came from, I was fooled. First of all, the room is very small, and the curtains have to be drawn all day, because it is next to the adjacent building and facing the window. The most incomprehensible thing is that there is no door in the bathroom, and the toilet is facing the bed. Was this designed by a designer from that country? The facilities are simple and the sanitation is not good. The breakfast is very poor, with few varieties and poor quality, and the attitude of the restaurant service staff is not good. Such a variety, there is no cost performance at all.
